## <a name="windows-server-2008-r2-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="7c5c6-1423">Atributos do Windows Server 2008 R2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7c5c6-1423">Windows Server 2008 R2 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7c5c6-1424">Essa classe contém os seguintes atributos para o Windows Server 2008 R2:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7c5c6-1424">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2008 R2:</span></span>
